 yah company kaa pehla smartphone he jisamen teen rier camere die gaye hai
 Its price starts at Rs 23,990
 iske do verient hai
 4GB RAM and 64GB internal memory, 128GB internal memory with 6GB RAM is given in the second variant
 is verient kii keemat 28,990 rupee he
 This smartphone can be purchased from Flipkart, Samsung online store and Samsung Oprah House on September 27-28
 iske baad yah ofline retail stores main bhi milegaa
 The Galaxy A7 has a 6-inch Full HD Plus Super AMOLED display
 yah smartphone samsung ke in house procesar octacor Exynos 7885 par chalata he
 Display Aspect Ratio 18
 5:9 kaa he or isamen gorilla glass 3 kii protection di gai he
 Android 8 in this device
 0oreoaxariwa samsung experience yujar interphes diya gaya he
 You will not see a fingerprint scanner in this smartphone, as it is placed on the side with the power button
 photography ke liye Galaxy A7 ke rier main tripalcameramodul diya gaya he
 One of these sensors is a 24-megapixel aperture f / 1
 7 he, doosraa 8 megapixl kaa ultra wide sensor he jiskaa aparchar f / 2
 There is 4 and the third is the depth sensor which is 5 megapixels
 iskaa aparchar f / 2
 Is 2 selfi ke liye is smartphone main elidi flash ke saath 24 megapixl kaa front camera diya gaya he
 The front camera supports live focus and pro lighting mode, under which studio lighting, filters and AR emoji have been provided
 samsung ke mutabik isse kam lite main acchhee photography hogi
 The given camera has a Scene Optimizer feature that adjusts camera settings by detecting senareos themselves, using Artificial Intelligence
 Galaxy A7 main 3,300 mah kii bydaree di gai he
 It has wifi, Bluetooth 5 for connectivity
 0, jeepies, headphone jaik ke saath yuasabi tip si jaise standard fitures die gaye hai

 sonia ne apane patr main kaha he ki aapke paas bahumat he mahila aarakshan bill ko loksabhaa main lie
 Congress will support the bill
 20 sitambar ko likhe patr main congress adhyaksh ne pradhanmantri se kaha he ki mahila aarakshan bill rajyasabha main paas ho chukaa he
 The BJP has a lot in the Lok Sabha
 aap isko paas karaie
 The results of the assembly elections held in Madhya Pradesh have been reached
 yahaan devatalab vidhansabha seat par bhartiya janata party (bijepi) ke girish gautam or congress ke vidyavati patel ke bich muqabla tha
 Here BJP candidate Girish Gautam managed to win with 45043 votes
 duusare sthaan par bahujan samaaj party kii seemaa senger raheen
 He received 43963 votes
 vahiin, congress kii vidyavati patel tisare sthaan par raheen
 He received 30383 votes
 maaloom ho ki reva jile ke is brahman bahulya is ilaake main kareeb 2 lakh voter hai
 Apart from this, obcs and Scheduled Castes also live in large numbers in the area
 vaise to yah bijepi kii paramparaagat seat rahi he lekin basapa or congress jaisi party bhi yahaan janaadhar rakhti hai
 In the 2013 elections, the situation was the same as in 2008, because even then there was a contest between Girish Gautam of BJP and Vidyavati Patel of BSP but in the results BJP won by 3885 votes
 congress kareeb 30 hajaar voton ke saath tisare number kii party thi or sapa ne bhi is seat se chunaav ladaa tha
 In 2008, bjp's Girish Gautam defeated bsp's Vidyavati by 3764 votes
 is chunaav main congress paanchaven sthaan par rahi or use nirdaleey pratyaashee se bhi kam kareeb 8 fisadi vot hi hasil hue the
 What was the assembly in 2013? Out of 230 seats in Madhya Pradesh Assembly, 35 seats are reserved for Scheduled Castes and 47 seats for Scheduled Tribes
 148 gaiyr-arakshit siten hai
 In the 2013 assembly elections, BJP won 165 seats and formed the government for the third consecutive time in the state, while the Congress had to satisfy itself with 58 seats

 According to the new safety regulations, since April 1, 2019, it is mandatory for two-wheelers with more than 125cc engines to have ABS as standard and two-wheelers with less than 125cc engines as standard
 jahaan ek taraf royal enfield kii sari bikes main dual-channel ABS system diya gaya he to vahiin Bullet 350 or 350 ES main single-channel ABS unit diya gaya he
 The dual channel ABS system monitors both the wheels during braking and prevents slipping, while the single-channel ABS does the same in only one wheel to which it is mounted, which is usually the front wheel

 ‘kargil vijay diwas', hamaare kritagya raashtra ke liye 1999 main kargil kii chotiyon par apane sashastr balon kii veerta kaa samaran karne kaa din he
 On this occasion, we salute the patience and valor of the warriors defending India
 ham sabhi shaheedon ke prati aaajeevan rini rahenge
 Jai Hind! xxrep 8 ? In a tweet made earlier, PM Modi said, 'I offer my heartfelt condolences to all the brave sons of Mother Bharati on Kargil Vijay Divas
 yah diwas hamen apane sainikon ke saahas, shaury or samarpan kii yaad dilaataa he
 On this occasion, my humble tribute to the mighty warriors who sacrificed their all in defense of the motherland
 jai hind!' pradhanmantri ne is twit ke saath ek video bhi share kiya he
 India had won the Kargil War on 26 July 1999
 kargil yuddh main bharat kii jeet ke baad se har saal 26 july ko kargil vijay diwas (kargil Vijay Diwas) manaaya jaataa aa rahaa he
 This day is celebrated to honor the soldiers who were martyred in the Kargil war
 kargil yuddh, jise oparation vijay ke naam se bhi janaa jaataa he, bharat or pakistan ke bich may or july 1999 ke bich kashmir ke kargil jile main hue sashastr sangharsh kaa naam he
 The Kargil War lasted for about 60 days and ended on 26 July
 bhartiya sena or vayusena ne pakistan ke kabze vaali jagahon par hamalaa kiya or dhire-dhire antarrashtriya sahyog se pakistan ko seemaa paar vaapis jane ko majaboor kiya
 This war took place on high altitude and the armies of both the countries had to face a lot of difficulty in fighting
 pakistani ghuspaithiyon ke khilaaf sena kii ore se kii gai karrwai main bhartiya sena ke 527 jawan shahid hue to kareeb 1363 ghayal hue the
 About three thousand soldiers of Pakistan were killed in this battle, but Pakistan believes that only about 357 of its soldiers were killed
 kargil yuddh bhartiya sena ke saahas or jambaaji kaa aisa udhaaharan he jis par har deshvasi ko garv hona chahie
 The prosecution received a major setback in the court on Wednesday in the much-publicized case of the 45-year-old man allegedly locking his wife's vagina due to doubts over the life-partner's character
 is maamle main peedit mahila apane pati ke khilaaf lagaae gaye sangeen aaropon se inkaar karte hue khud ke puraane bayanon se mukar gai jiske baad use mukari hui gavaah ghoshit kar diya gaya
 The woman appeared in the court of Additional Sessions Judge Avanindra Kumar Singh as a prosecution witness
 vah nyaayadhish ke saamne na keval police ko die bayaan se mukar gai, balki usne apane us kathan se bhi inkaar kar diya jo usne dand prakriya samhita (siarpisi) kii dhara 164 ke tahat adaalat main darj karaayaa tha
 The woman said, 'I do not know what statement i (to the police) made, because i was hospitalized at that time
 mujhe hosh nahin he ki maine police ko bayaan diya tha yaa nahin
 'she said,' i did not even say in court that my husband had locked my genitals on suspicion
 ’ The woman said, "I have not made any such statement in the court that when my husband goes to work, i lock my penis and when i come back it opens it
" ’ The mother of five, however, told the court that her husband Sohanlal (45), who works in a garage, used to fight and fight her over trivial matters
 lekin usne apane chote bacchon kii parvarish kii chintaa karte hue pati ke khilaaf kahin koi shikaayat nahin kii
 Relying on the police investigation, for a long time, the woman, who has been facing the alleged cruelty of her husband, tried suicide on 16 July 2012 by drinking a rat drug
 lekin mahila ne aatmahatya ke prayaas ke peeche is vajah se adaalat main saaf inkaar kar diya
 She said that she had a dispute with her husband over the 'trivial matter' of withdrawing money and that he got angry and drank poison
 mahila ke apane puraane bayanon se mukarne ke baad adaalat ne abhiyojan paksh kii guzarish par use mukari hui gavaah ghoshit karne kii anumati de di
 However, the prosecution was strengthened by the testimony of a gynecologist of the city's governing Maharaja Yashwantrao Hospital (MYH)
 emvyech kii dow vibha maujes ne adaalat ko bataaya ki unhone 16 july 2012 ko aspataal main mahila ke ilaaj ke dauraan peshaab kii nalee lagaate samay dekha ki uske guptang par taala laga he
 The comments dow vibha ne kaha, ‘jab is taale ke bare main marij se jaankaree lee gai, to usne bataaya ki uske pati ne chaar saal pehle use ganja pilaakar behosh kar diya tha
 After this, he was punched by a screwdriver and locked his genitals
 ’ abhiyojan kii gavaah ne bataaya ki usne police kii muhaiyaa karai gai chaabi se mahila ke guptang par laga taala kholaa
 The woman's husband is currently in jail under judicial custody
 us par bhartiya dand vidhaan (ipisi) kii dhara 498-k (patni par pati kii krurta), dhara 326 (khatarnaak hathiyaaron se gambhir chot pahunchaana) or dhara 344 (bandhak banaakar rakhana) ke tahat mukadmaa chal rahaa he
 In this case, the aggrieved woman refuted the old allegations against her husband and denied the old statements of her own, after which she was declared a defunct witness
 yah mahila apper satr nyaayadhish avaneendra kumaar singh kii adaalat main abhiyojan kii gavaah ke rup main pesh hui thi
 She not only turned down a statement to the police before the judge, but also denied her statement which she had lodged in the court under section 164 of the Criminal Procedure Code (CRPC)
 mahila ne kaha, ‘mujhe nahin maaloom ki maine (police ko) kya bayaan diya tha, kyonki main us vakt aspataal main bhartee thi
 i am not aware whether i gave a statement to the police or not
 ’ usne kaha, ‘maine adaalat main yah bhi nahin kaha ki mere pati ne shaq kii bina par mere guptang par taala laga diya tha
 ' mahila ne kaha, ‘maine adaalat main aisa koi bayaan nahin diya ki meraa pati jab kaam par jaataa he, to mere yonang par taala laga detaa he or waapas aane par yah taala khol detaa he
 ' paanch bacchon kii maa ne haalanki adaalat ko bataaya ki ek garrej main kaam karne vaala uskaa pati sohanlal (45) choti-choti baton ko lekar usase jhagada or marpet karata tha
 But she did not complain against her husband, worrying about raising her young children
 police kii jaanch par bharosa karen, to lambe vakt se apane pati kii kathith krurta jhel rahi mahila ne 16 july 2012 ko chuuhe maarane vaali dawa pikar khudakushi kii koshish kii thi
 But the woman flatly refused in court because of the reason behind the suicide attempt
 usne kaha ki paise nikaalane kii ‘choti-si baat par’ uskaa pati se vivaad hua tha or usne gusse main aakar jehar pi liya tha
 After the woman turned away from her old statements, the court allowed the prosecution to declare her as a defunct witness
 baharhaal, shahar ke shaskeey maharaja yashwantrao aspataal (emvyech) kii ek stri rog visheshgy kii gavaahi se abhiyojan paksh ko bal mila
 Dr
 Vibha Mauges of MYH told the court that on July 16, 2012, while treating the woman in the hospital while urinating, she noticed that her genitals were locked
 tippaniyan Dr
 Vibha said, "when information was taken from the patient about this lock, she told that her husband had made her unconscious after drinking cannabis four years ago
 iske baad penchkas (scru driver) se chhed karke uske guptang par taala laga diya tha
 The prosecution witness said that he opened the lock on the woman's genitals with the key provided by the police
 mahila kaa pati philhal nyaayik hiraasat ke tahat jail main band he
 He is being tried under Section 498-A (cruelty of husband on wife), Section 326 (causing serious injury to dangerous weapons) and Section 344 (holding hostage) of Indian Penal Code (IPC)
